***verstoppertje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verstoppertje.html>verstoppertje</a> (10209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i><a href = vnd.unilang:verstoppen.html>verstoppen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verstoppertje.html>verstoppertje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)

***vert.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a> (97718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">viridis</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">virid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">verts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A green colour, now only in heraldry; represented in engraving by diagonal parallel lines 45 degrees counter-clockwise.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Green undergrowth or other vegetation growing in a forest, as a potential cover for deer.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The right to fell trees or cut shrubs in a forest.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1819</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Scott,  <cite>Ivanhoe</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“I understand <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a>,” <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> the King, “and the Holy Clerk shall have a grant of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a></b> and venison in my woods of Warncliffe.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In blazon, of the colour green.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">verdant</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Abbreviation of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">vertical</i></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:vert.html>vert</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">verts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In sport, a type of bicycle <a href = vnd.unilang:stunt.html>stunt</a> competition.</li>
<li>A vertical surface used by <a href = vnd.unilang:skateboarders.html>skateboarders</a> or skiers.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Abbreviation of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">vertebrate</i></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> vertebrate</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vertellen.html>vertellen</a></i>. </p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verteld.html>verteld</a></b>. / <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertelde.html>vertelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I have <b><a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a></b> him. / I <b><a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a></b> him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervaldatum.html>vervaldatum</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervaldatum.html>vervaldata</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervaldatums.html>vervaldatums</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>due date (of payment)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> before date</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervallen.html>vervallen</a> (10952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervallen.html>vervallen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to decline, reject</li>
<li>to worsen</li>
<li>to decay, <a href = vnd.unilang:rot.html>rot</a></li>
<li>to recede, pull away</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cease to be valid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of food</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expire</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>dilapidated, ruinous</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of food</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> expired</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervanger.html>vervanger</a></i>. ***vervelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervelen.html>vervelen</a> (5989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervelen.html>vervelen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become or seem to be too much</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervelen.html>vervelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to annoy, to pester</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:boren.html>bore</a>; inspire boredom in somebody</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be bored</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verveel.html>verveel</a></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervelend.html>vervelend</a> (1914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
